
# BARS - MEDIUM
#   setup (color, type)
#   colors
#   start, 10s, 5, 1s, end

defined_text = {
	name = ttt_BarM1
	random = no
	text = {
		localisation_key = ttt_barM1
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = ttt_barM1
		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = ttt_barM1
		trigger = {
			has_province_flag = ttt_barM1
		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = ttt_none
	}
}
defined_text = {
	name = ttt_BarM1Color
	random = no
	text = {
		localisation_key = ttt_GbarM1
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				is_variable_equal = { which = ttt_barM1_color value = 1 }
				is_variable_equal = { which = ttt_barM1_color value = -1 }
			}
		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = ttt_RbarM1
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				is_variable_equal = { which = ttt_barM1_color value = 2 }
				is_variable_equal = { which = ttt_barM1_color value = -2 }
			}
		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = ttt_BbarM1
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				is_variable_equal = { which = ttt_barM1_color value = 3 }
				is_variable_equal = { which = ttt_barM1_color value = -3 }
			}
		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = ttt_YbarM1
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				is_variable_equal = { which = ttt_barM1_color value = 4 }
				is_variable_equal = { which = ttt_barM1_color value = -4 }
			}
		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = ttt_none
	}
}

	name = ttt_BarM1_frame

		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = ttt_barM_framebg
	}
}

	}

	name = ttt_BarS1Color
	random = no
	text = {
		localisation_key = ttt_GbarS1
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				is_variable_equal = { which = ttt_barS1_color value = 1 }
				is_variable_equal = { which = ttt_barS1_color value = -1 }
			}
		}
	}

	name = ttt_BarS3
	random = no
	text = {
		localisation_key = ttt_barS3
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = ttt_barS3
		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = ttt_barS3
		trigger = {
			has_province_flag = ttt_barS3
		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = ttt_none
	}
}
defined_text = {
	name = ttt_BarS3Color
	random = no
	text = {
		localisation_key = ttt_GbarS3
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				is_variable_equal = { which = ttt_barS3_color value = 1 }
				is_variable_equal = { which = ttt_barS3_color value = -1 }
			}
		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = ttt_RbarS3
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				is_variable_equal = { which = ttt_barS3_color value = 2 }
				is_variable_equal = { which = ttt_barS3_color value = -2 }
			}
		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = ttt_BbarS3
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				is_variable_equal = { which = ttt_barS3_color value = 3 }
				is_variable_equal = { which = ttt_barS3_color value = -3 }
			}
		}
	}

		localisation_key = ttt_YbarS3

	name = ttt_BarS4
	random = no
	text = {
		localisation_key = ttt_barS4
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = ttt_barS4
		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = ttt_barS4
		trigger = {
			has_province_flag = ttt_barS4
		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = ttt_none
	}
}
defined_text = {
	name = ttt_BarS4Color
	random = no
	text = {
		localisation_key = ttt_GbarS4
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				is_variable_equal = { which = ttt_barS4_color value = 1 }
				is_variable_equal = { which = ttt_barS4_color value = -1 }
			}
		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = ttt_RbarS4
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				is_variable_equal = { which = ttt_barS4_color value = 2 }
				is_variable_equal = { which = ttt_barS4_color value = -2 }
			}
		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = ttt_BbarS4
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				is_variable_equal = { which = ttt_barS4_color value = 3 }

			}
		}

			has_country_flag = ttt_barS5
		}

	}

	name = ttt_BarS5Color
	random = no
	text = {
		localisation_key = ttt_GbarS5
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				is_variable_equal = { which = ttt_barS5_color value = 1 }
				is_variable_equal = { which = ttt_barS5_color value = -1 }
			}
		}

	name = ttt_BarL1
	random = no
	text = {
		localisation_key = ttt_barL1
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = ttt_barL1
		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = ttt_barL1
		trigger = {
			has_province_flag = ttt_barL1
		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = ttt_none
	}
}
defined_text = {
	name = ttt_BarL1Color
	random = no
	text = {
		localisation_key = ttt_GbarL1
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				is_variable_equal = { which = ttt_barL1_color value = 1 }
				is_variable_equal = { which = ttt_barL1_color value = -1 }
			}
		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = ttt_RbarL1
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				is_variable_equal = { which = ttt_barL1_color value = 2 }
				is_variable_equal = { which = ttt_barL1_color value = -2 }
			}
		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = ttt_BbarL1
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				is_variable_equal = { which = ttt_barL1_color value = 3 }
				is_variable_equal = { which = ttt_barL1_color value = -3 }
			}
		}
	}

		localisation_key = ttt_YbarL1

# BarL 2


defined_text = {
	name = ttt_BarL2
	random = no
	text = {
		localisation_key = ttt_barL2
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = ttt_barL2
		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = ttt_barL2
		trigger = {
			has_province_flag = ttt_barL2
		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = ttt_none
	}
}
defined_text = {
	name = ttt_BarL2Color
	random = no
	text = {
		localisation_key = ttt_GbarL2
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				is_variable_equal = { which = ttt_barL2_color value = 1 }
				is_variable_equal = { which = ttt_barL2_color value = -1 }
			}
		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = ttt_RbarL2
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				is_variable_equal = { which = ttt_barL2_color value = 2 }
				is_variable_equal = { which = ttt_barL2_color value = -2 }
			}
		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = ttt_BbarL2
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				is_variable_equal = { which = ttt_barL2_color value = 3 }
				is_variable_equal = { which = ttt_barL2_color value = -3 }
			}
		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = ttt_YbarL2
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				is_variable_equal = { which = ttt_barL2_color value = 4 }
				is_variable_equal = { which = ttt_barL2_color value = -4 }
			}
		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = ttt_none
	}
}

	name = ttt_BarL2_frame
	random = no

		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = ttt_barL_framebg
	}
}

defined_text = {
	name = ttt_BarL4Color
	random = no
	text = {
		localisation_key = ttt_GbarL4
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				is_variable_equal = { which = ttt_barL4_color value = 1 }
				is_variable_equal = { which = ttt_barL4_color value = -1 }
			}
		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = ttt_RbarL4
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				is_variable_equal = { which = ttt_barL4_color value = 2 }
				is_variable_equal = { which = ttt_barL4_color value = -2 }
			}
		}

defined_text = {
	name = ttt_BarL5
	random = no
	text = {
		localisation_key = ttt_barL5
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = ttt_barL5
		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = ttt_barL5
		trigger = {
			has_province_flag = ttt_barL5
		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = ttt_none
	}
}
defined_text = {
	name = ttt_BarL5Color
	random = no
	text = {
		localisation_key = ttt_GbarL5
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				is_variable_equal = { which = ttt_barL5_color value = 1 }
				is_variable_equal = { which = ttt_barL5_color value = -1 }
			}
		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = ttt_RbarL5
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				is_variable_equal = { which = ttt_barL5_color value = 2 }
				is_variable_equal = { which = ttt_barL5_color value = -2 }
			}
		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = ttt_BbarL5
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				is_variable_equal = { which = ttt_barL5_color value = 3 }
				is_variable_equal = { which = ttt_barL5_color value = -3 }
			}
		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = ttt_YbarL5

				is_variable_equal = { which = ttt_barX2_color value = -1 }
			}
		}

# BarX 4


defined_text = {
	name = ttt_BarX4
	random = no
	text = {
		localisation_key = ttt_barX4
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = ttt_barX4
		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = ttt_barX4
		trigger = {
			has_province_flag = ttt_barX4
		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = ttt_none
	}
}
defined_text = {
	name = ttt_BarX4Color
	random = no
	text = {
		localisation_key = ttt_GbarX4
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				is_variable_equal = { which = ttt_barX4_color value = 1 }
				is_variable_equal = { which = ttt_barX4_color value = -1 }
			}
		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = ttt_RbarX4
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				is_variable_equal = { which = ttt_barX4_color value = 2 }
				is_variable_equal = { which = ttt_barX4_color value = -2 }
			}
		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = ttt_BbarX4
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				is_variable_equal = { which = ttt_barX4_color value = 3 }
				is_variable_equal = { which = ttt_barX4_color value = -3 }
			}
		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = ttt_YbarX4
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				is_variable_equal = { which = ttt_barX4_color value = 4 }
				is_variable_equal = { which = ttt_barX4_color value = -4 }
			}
		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = ttt_none
	}

		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = ttt_barX5
		}
	}

		localisation_key = ttt_barX5
		trigger = {
			has_province_flag = ttt_barX5
		}

		localisation_key = ttt_none
	}

defined_text = {
	name = ttt_BarX5Color
	random = no
	text = {
		localisation_key = ttt_GbarX5
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				is_variable_equal = { which = ttt_barX5_color value = 1 }
				is_variable_equal = { which = ttt_barX5_color value = -1 }
			}
		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = ttt_RbarX5
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				is_variable_equal = { which = ttt_barX5_color value = 2 }
				is_variable_equal = { which = ttt_barX5_color value = -2 }
			}
		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = ttt_BbarX5
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				is_variable_equal = { which = ttt_barX5_color value = 3 }
				is_variable_equal = { which = ttt_barX5_color value = -3 }
			}
		}
